    40	export class QuestionRowModel extends Base {
    41	  protected _scrollableParent: any = undefined;
    42	  protected _updateVisibility: any = undefined;
    43	  private get allowRendering(): boolean {
    44	    return !this.panel || !this.panel.survey || !(this.panel.survey as any)["isLazyRenderingSuspended"];
    45	  }
    46	  private lazyRenderingTimeout: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>;
    47	  public startLazyRendering(rowContainerDiv: HTMLElement, findScrollableContainer = findScrollableParent): void {
    48	    if (!DomDocumentHelper.isAvailable()) return;
    49	    this._scrollableParent = findScrollableContainer(rowContainerDiv);
    50	    // if  this._scrollableParent is html the scroll event isn't fired, so we should use window
    51	    if (this._scrollableParent === DomDocumentHelper.getDocumentElement()) {
    52	      this._scrollableParent = DomWindowHelper.getWindow();
    53	    }
    54	    const hasScroll = this._scrollableParent.scrollHeight > this._scrollableParent.clientHeight;
    55	    this.isNeedRender = !hasScroll;
    56	    if (hasScroll) {
    57	      this._updateVisibility = () => {
    58	        if (!this.allowRendering) {
    59	          return;
    60	        }
    61	        var isRowContainerDivVisible = isElementVisible(rowContainerDiv, 50);
    62	        if (!this.isNeedRender && isRowContainerDivVisible) {
    63	          this.isNeedRender = true;
    64	          this.stopLazyRendering();
    65	        }
    66	      };
    67	      this.lazyRenderingTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
    68	        if (
    69	          !!this._scrollableParent &&
    70	          !!this._scrollableParent.addEventListener
    71	        ) {
    72	          this._scrollableParent.addEventListener(
    73	            "scroll",
    74	            this._updateVisibility
    75	          );
    76	        }
    77	        this.ensureVisibility();
    78	      }, 10);
    79	    }
    80	  }
    81	  public ensureVisibility() {
    82	    if (!!this._updateVisibility) {
    83	      this._updateVisibility();
    84	    }
    85	  }
    86	  public stopLazyRendering() {
    87	    if (
    88	      !!this._scrollableParent &&
    89	      !!this._updateVisibility &&
    90	      !!this._scrollableParent.removeEventListener
    91	    ) {
    92	      this._scrollableParent.removeEventListener(
    93	        "scroll",
    94	        this._updateVisibility
    95	      );
    96	    }
    97	    clearTimeout(this.lazyRenderingTimeout);
    98	    this._scrollableParent = undefined;
    99	    this._updateVisibility = undefined;
   100	  }
   101	  constructor(public panel: PanelModelBase) {

   133	  private getVisibleElementsAnimationOptions(): IAnimationGroupConsumer<IElement> {

   167	  public set visibleElements(val: Array<IElement>) {

   180	  public onVisibleChangedCallback: () => void;
   181	  @property({ defaultValue: true }) visible: boolean;
   182	  @property() isNeedRender: boolean;
   183	
   184	  public updateVisible() {
   185	    var visElements: Array<IElement> = [];
   186	    for (var i = 0; i < this.elements.length; i++) {
   187	      if (this.elements[i].isVisible) {
   188	        visElements.push(this.elements[i]);
   189	      }
   190	      if (this.elements[i].isPanel || this.elements[i].getType() === "paneldynamic") {
   191	        this.setIsLazyRendering(false);
   192	        this.stopLazyRendering();
   193	      }
   194	    }
   195	    this.visibleElements = visElements;
   196	    return;
   197	  }
   198	  public addElement(q: IElement) {
   199	    this.elements.push(q);
   200	    this.updateVisible();
   201	  }
   202	  public get index(): number {
   203	    return this.panel.rows.indexOf(this);
   204	  }
   205	  private setWidth(visibleElement: Array<IElement>) {
   206	    var visCount = visibleElement.length;
   207	    if (visCount == 0) return;
   208	    const isSingleInRow = visibleElement.length === 1;
   209	    var counter = 0;
   210	    var preSetWidthElements = [];
   211	    for (var i = 0; i < this.elements.length; i++) {
   212	      var el = this.elements[i];
   213	
   214	      if (el.isVisible) {
   215	        (<any>el).isSingleInRow = isSingleInRow;
   216	        var width = this.getElementWidth(el);
   217	        if (!!width) {
   218	          el.renderWidth = this.getRenderedWidthFromWidth(width);
   219	          preSetWidthElements.push(el);
   220	        }
   221	        el.rightIndent = 0;
   222	        counter++;
   223	      } else {
   224	        el.renderWidth = "";
   225	      }
   226	    }
   227	    for (var i = 0; i < this.elements.length; i++) {
   228	      var el = this.elements[i];
   229	      if (!el.isVisible || preSetWidthElements.indexOf(el) > -1) continue;
   230	      if (preSetWidthElements.length == 0) {
   231	        el.renderWidth = `${Number.parseFloat((100 / visCount).toFixed(6))}%`;
   232	      } else {
   233	        el.renderWidth = this.getRenderedCalcWidth(
   234	          el,
   235	          preSetWidthElements,
   236	          visCount
   237	        );
   238	      }
   239	    }
   240	  }
   241	
   242	  private getRenderedCalcWidth(
   243	    el: IElement,
   244	    preSetWidthElements: Array<IElement>,
   245	    visCount: number
   246	  ): string {
   247	    var expression = "100%";
   248	    for (var i = 0; i < preSetWidthElements.length; i++) {
   249	      expression += " - " + preSetWidthElements[i].renderWidth;
   250	    }
   251	    var calcWidthEl = visCount - preSetWidthElements.length;
   252	    if (calcWidthEl > 1) {
   253	      expression = "(" + expression + ")/" + calcWidthEl.toString();
   254	    }
   255	    return "calc(" + expression + ")";
   256	  }
   257	  private getElementWidth(el: IElement): string {
   258	    var width = el.width;
   259	    if (!width || typeof width !== "string") return "";
   260	    return width.trim();
   261	  }
   262	  private getRenderedWidthFromWidth(width: string): string {
   263	    return Helpers.isNumber(width) ? width + "px" : width;
   264	  }
   265	  public dispose(): void {
   266	    super.dispose();

   268	  }

   275	      .toString();
   276	  }

  1028	    }

  1031	      this.updateContainsErrors();
  1032	    }
  1033	  }

import { SurveyModel } from "./packages/survey-core/src/survey";
import { PanelModel } from "./packages/survey-core/src/panel";
import { settings } from "./packages/survey-core/src/settings";

// Test 1: Panel that is readOnly and isRequired should not show required errors
const survey = new SurveyModel({
  "pages": [
    {
      "name": "page1",
      "elements": [
        {
          "type": "panel",
          "name": "panel1",
          "readOnly": true,
          "title": "Required Panel",
          "isRequired": true,
          "elements": [
            {
              "type": "text",
              "name": "question1"
            }
          ]
        }
      ]
    }
  ]
});

console.log("Panel isReadOnly:", panel.isReadOnly);
console.log("Panel isRequired:", panel.isRequired);

// Run validation

All edge cases pass. Now let me also check if the `hasRequiredError` method in `question.ts` should be updated to also consider readOnly for consistency:

Looking at the code flow:
1. `validateElement` → `canCollectErrors` (checks `!this.isReadOnly || settings.readOnly.enableValidation`) → `collectErrors` → `onCheckForErrors` → `hasRequiredError`

So `hasRequiredError` is only reached if `canCollectErrors` returns true. If the question is read-only, `canCollectErrors` returns false (unless `settings.readOnly.enableValidation` is true), so `hasRequiredError` is never called. This is correct.

But `hasRequiredError` is a public method. Someone could call it directly. Should we add the check there too? Let me check if it's used elsewhere:

- `question_imagepicker.ts:460` uses it for `ariaRequired` attribute - this is about accessibility, not validation. For accessibility, a read-only required field should probably still be marked as required for screen readers. So this is fine.

I think the main fix is in `panel.ts` which I've already made. But let me also check if the `hasRequiredError` in `question.ts` should be updated for safety:

Actually, looking at the PR description title: "Skip 'required' validation when a question is read-only (or has a read-only parent)". It mentions both panels and questions. The question case already works because of `canCollectErrors`. But what if someone calls `hasRequiredError` directly? Let me add the check there too for consistency.





🎬 ACTION

    return this.isRequired && this.isEmpty();
  }' --new_str 'public hasRequiredError(): boolean {
    return this.isRequired && this.isEmpty() && (!this.isReadOnly || settings.readOnly.enableValidation);
  }'

const { SurveyModel, settings } = require('./packages/survey-core/build/survey.core.js');

// Final comprehensive verification
let allPass = true;

function test(name, condition) {
  console.log(name + ':', condition ? 'PASS' : 'FAIL');
  if (!condition) allPass = false;
}

// Main scenario from PR
const s1 = new SurveyModel({
  'pages': [{'name': 'page1', 'elements': [
    {'type': 'panel', 'name': 'panel1', 'readOnly': true, 'title': 'Required Panel', 'isRequired': true,
     'elements': [{'type': 'text', 'name': 'question1'}]}
  ]}]
});
s1.validate();
test('PR scenario: readOnly panel + isRequired shows no errors', s1.getPanelByName('panel1').errors.length === 0);

// Question variant
const s2 = new SurveyModel({
  'pages': [{'name': 'page1', 'elements': [
    {'type': 'text', 'name': 'q1', 'readOnly': true, 'isRequired': true}
  ]}]
});
s2.validate();
test('readOnly question + isRequired shows no errors', s2.getQuestionByName('q1').errors.length === 0);

// Parent readOnly
const s3 = new SurveyModel({
  'pages': [{'name': 'page1', 'elements': [
    {'type': 'panel', 'name': 'outer', 'readOnly': true, 'elements': [
      {'type': 'panel', 'name': 'inner', 'isRequired': true, 'elements': [
        {'type': 'text', 'name': 'q2'}
      ]}
    ]}
  ]}]
});
s3.validate();
test('Panel with readOnly parent + isRequired shows no errors', s3.getPanelByName('inner').errors.length === 0);

// Normal cases still work
const s4 = new SurveyModel({
  'pages': [{'name': 'page1', 'elements': [
    {'type': 'panel', 'name': 'p4', 'isRequired': true, 'elements': [{'type': 'text', 'name': 'q4'}]}
  ]}]
});
s4.validate();
test('Normal required panel still validates', s4.getPanelByName('p4').errors.length === 1);

const s5 = new SurveyModel({
  'pages': [{'name': 'page1', 'elements': [
    {'type': 'text', 'name': 'q5', 'isRequired': true}
  ]}]
});
s5.validate();
test('Normal required question still validates', s5.getQuestionByName('q5').errors.length === 1);

// enableValidation flag
settings.readOnly.enableValidation = true;
const s6 = new SurveyModel({
  'pages': [{'name': 'page1', 'elements': [
    {'type': 'panel', 'name': 'p6', 'readOnly': true, 'isRequired': true, 'elements': [{'type': 'text', 'name': 'q6'}]}
  ]}]
});
s6.validate();
test('readOnly + enableValidation=true still validates', s6.getPanelByName('p6').errors.length === 1);
settings.readOnly.enableValidation = false;

console.log('');
console.log('All tests passed:', allPass);
"
